Eczacıbaşı Information and Communication Technologies (Eczacıbaşı ICT) is a provider of information technology solutions and services with more than 25 years of experience.

Eczacıbaşı ICT has two main technology and managed services areas providing comprehensive solutions for applications support and development services as well as for infrastructure and managed services. The business units in each area cover specific areas of expertise from e-signature solutions, portals (Microsoft SharePoint, IBM WebSphere), knowledge and business process management solutions, mobile application development, customer relationship management solutions, ERP, Business Intelligence consulting services, data center operations, network and security operations, virtualization solutions to disaster recovery and business recovery services.">

    <section class="core-section-container
        core-section-container--with-border border-b-1 border-solid border-color-border-faint py-4 text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us">
<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Eczacıbaşı Information and Communication Technologies

Eczacıbaşı Information and Communication Technologies (Eczacıbaşı ICT) is a provider of information technology solutions and services with more than 25 years of experience.

Eczacıbaşı ICT has two main technology and managed services areas providing comprehensive solutions for applications support and development services as well as for infrastructure and managed services. The business units in each area cover specific areas of expertise from e-signature solutions, portals (Microsoft SharePoint, IBM WebSphere), knowledge and business process management solutions, mobile application development, customer relationship management solutions, ERP, Business Intelligence consulting services, data center operations, network and security operations, virtualization solutions to disaster recovery and business recovery services.

Data Center Management

Eczacıbaşı ICT has one of the largest and most sophisticated data centers in Turkey, where it hosts more than 1000+ servers belonging to internal and external customers. It also runs data centers for the authorized electronic security certificate provider E-Guven and Turkcell’s 7x24 mobile signature operation.

Software and Solutions

Eczacıbaşı ICT maintains an expertise in all new industry technologies and processes, such as Cloud Technologies and new offerings in IaaS (Infrastructure as a Service), PaaS (Platform as a Service), SaaS (Software as a Service) and Shared Service Centers (SSC). Another area the company has focused on, and where it is the first in Turkey, is SaaS HR Management tools and systems for small and medium-sized clients.

While successfully providing many outsourcing services to clients, Eczacıbaşı ICT is also developing innovative products or services.
          </p>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary"><a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/company/eczacibasi-toplulugu?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Eczacıbaşı Topluluğu</a> CIO'su <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/hilmi-kocak-41240b5?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Hilmi Kocak</a>, “Türkiye’nin Değer Yaratan 50 CTO’su” arasında yer aldı. BUSINESS LIFE için bu yılın başında Zenna araştırma şirketinin gerçekleştirdiği “Türkiye’nin En İyi Yönetilen Şirketleri” araştırmasında öne çıkan kurumların CTO’ları da bu araştırmada öne çıktı. Türkiye’nin Değer Yaratan 50 CTO’su araştırması, sektörde öncü ve yenilikçi adımlar atarak değer yaratanlara odaklandı. Dergimizin yayın kurulu ve seçici kurul üyelerinin katkılarıyla şekillenen listemizde değer yaratanlar yenilikçi adımlarıyla da yer aldı. 

Araştırmanın detayları <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/company/businesslifetr?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>BUSINESS LIFE</a> Eylül 2025 sayısında.
<a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dVy_EwxG?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dVy_EwxG</a></p>

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">📢 Yeni blog yayında!

Eczacıbaşı Bilişim Network Kıdemli Uzmanı <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/jihat-mazlum-olcay-1637b0226?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Jihat Mazlum Olcay</a>’ın kaleme aldığı bu yazıda, çok lokasyonlu ve hibrit çalışma düzeninde güvenli ve kesintisiz ağ altyapısının önemini ele alıyoruz.

7/24 izleme, güvenlik odaklı yaklaşım, performans optimizasyonu ve ölçeklenebilir çözümlerle kurumların ağ yönetimini nasıl kolaylaştırdığımızı keşfedin.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🔍 Eczacıbaşı Bilişim Ar-Ge Merkezi olarak, üniversite iş birlikleriyle yenilikçi çözümler üretmeye devam ediyoruz.
 
Ankara Üniversitesi ile yürüttüğümüz Oltalama Simülasyonu Ar-Ge projesi kapsamında, TÜBİTAK 1505 Üniversite-Sanayi İş Birliği Destek Programı başvurumuzun ilk hakem sunumunu başarıyla gerçekleştirdik.
Bu iş birliği, akademik bilgi birikimi ile sektör deneyimini bir araya getirerek ülkemizin siber güvenlik yetkinliğini güçlendirme hedefimizin önemli bir adımını oluşturuyor.
 
Proje sürecine katkı sağlayan <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/school/ankara-university/?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Ankara Üniversitesi</a> ekibine ve tüm çalışma arkadaşlarımıza teşekkür ederiz 👏

    <p class="linkedin-tc__text text-color-text-low-emphasis text-xs pb-2 contextual-sign-in-modal__terms-and-conditions m-auto w-[320px] pt-2 babybear:w-full" data-impression-id="linkedin-tc__button-skip-tc-text">
      Devam Et seçeneğini tıklayarak veya oturum açarak LinkedIn <a href="/legal/user-agreement?trk=linkedin-tc_auth-button_user-agreement" target="_blank" data-tracking-control-name="linkedin-tc_auth-button_user-agreement" data-tracking-will-navigate="true">Kullanıcı Anlaşması’nı</a>, <a href="/legal/privacy-policy?trk=linkedin-tc_auth-button_privacy-policy" target="_blank" data-tracking-control-name="linkedin-tc_auth-button_privacy-policy" data-tracking-will-navigate="true">Gizlilik Politikası’nı</a> ve <a href="/legal/cookie-policy?trk=linkedin-tc_auth-button_cookie-policy" target="_blank" data-tracking-control-name="linkedin-tc_auth-button_cookie-policy" data-tracking-will-navigate="true">Çerez Politikası’nı</a> kabul etmiş olursunuz.
    </p>
  
              </div>
